  @plex prop(key: keyof Props) {
    return this.props()[key];
  }

  protected propMap = new Map<keyof Props, Function>();

  prop2(key: keyof Props) {
    const value = this._props[key];
    let val = this.propMap.get(key);
    if (val) return val;

    val =
      typeof value === "function"
        ? (...args: unknown[]) => this.prop(key)(...args)
        : () => this.prop(key);
    this.propMap.set(key, val);

    return val;
  }

  @solo props(props = this._props) {
    this._props = props;
    return props;
  }
